"eos Canberra is located at the northern end of the Australian Capital Territory , 300 kilometres ( 190 mi ) southwest of Sydney , and 650 kilometres ( 400 mi ) north - east of Melbourne . The site of Canberra was selected for the location of the nation 's capital in 1908 as a compromise between Sydney and Melbourne , the two largest cities ."
"eos Canberra is unusual among Australian cities as an entirely purpose - built , planned city . Following an international contest for Canberra design , a design by Chicago architect Walter Burley Griffin was selected and construction commenced in 1913 ."
"eos Following an international contest for Canberra design , a design by Chicago architect Walter Burley Griffin was selected and construction commenced in 1913 . Although the growth and development of"
"eos Canberra design was heavily influenced by the garden city movement and incorporates significant areas of natural vegetation that have earned Canberra the title ` ` bush capital '' . "eos Canberra is also the location of several social and cultural institutions of national significance . The federal government contributes the largest percentage of Gross State Product and is the largest employer in Canberra ."

"eos Chief_Mountain is one of the most prominent peaks along the Rocky Mountain Front , a 200 mile ( 321 km ) long overthrust fault , known as the Lewis Overthrust , which extends from central Montana into southern Alberta , Canada . "eos Lava eruptions from Mauna_Loa are silica - poor , thus very fluid : and as a result eruptions tend to be non - explosive and Mauna_Loa has extremely shallow slopes . Mauna_Loa has probably been erupting for at least 700,000 years and Mauna_Loa may have emerged above sea level about 400,000 years ago , although the oldest - known dated rocks do not extend beyond 200,000 years ."
"eos Mauna_Loa most recent eruption occurred from march 24 1984 , to april 15 1984 . No recent eruptions of Mauna_Loa have caused fatalities , but eruptions in 1926 and 1950 destroyed villages , and the city of Hilo is partly built on lava flows from the late nineteenth century . "eos Mount_Etna ( also known as Muncibeddu in Sicilian and Mongibello in Italian , a combination of Latin mons and Arabic gibel , both meaning mountain ) is an active volcano on the east coast of Sicily , close to Messina and Catania ."

"eos Mount_Evans is often compared to Pikes Peak - another Front Range fourteener - which Mount_Evans exceeds in elevation by 154 ft ( 50 m ) . Mount_Evans was originally known as Mount Rosa or Mount Rosalie ( named for the wife of Fitz Hugh Ludlow who would later be the wife of Albert Bierstadt , and featured in Bierstadt 's painting ` ` Storm in the Rocky Mountains '' ) , and Mount_Evans is located in what is known by locals as the Chicago Peaks Range ."
"eos Mount_Evans is believed to have been climbed first in 1872 by Judge Lunt and a friend , but many accounts point to Albert Bierstadt as the first ascender in 1863 . In 1895 , Colorado 's legislature officially renamed Mount_Evans in honor of John Evans , second governor of the Colorado Territory from 1862 to 1865 ."

"eos Alan_Turing provided an influential formalisation of the concept of the algorithm and computation with the Turing machine , formulating the now widely accepted ` ` Turing '' version of the Church - Turing thesis , namely that any practical computing model has either the equivalent or a subset of the capabilities of a Turing machine . With the Turing test , Alan_Turing made a significant and characteristically provocative contribution to the debate regarding artificial intelligence : whether it will ever be possible to say that a machine is conscious and can think . "eos Rene_Descartes ( march 31 , 1596 - february 11 , 1650 ) , also known as Cartesius , was a noted French philosopher , mathematician , and scientist . Dubbed the ` ` Founder of Modern Philosophy '' and the ` ` Father of Modern Mathematics , '' Rene_Descartes ranks as one of the most important and influential thinkers of modern times . For good or bad , much of subsequent western philosophy is a reaction to Rene_Descartes writings , which have been closely studied from"
"eos For good or bad , much of subsequent western philosophy is a reaction to Rene_Descartes writings , which have been closely studied from Rene_Descartes time down to the present day . Rene_Descartes was one of the key thinkers of the Scientific Revolution in the Western World . Rene_Descartes influence in mathematics is also apparent , the Cartesian coordinate system used in plane geometry and algebra being named after"
"eos In the opening section of the ` ` Passions of the Soul '' , Rene_Descartes goes so far as to assert that Rene_Descartes will write on Rene_Descartes topic ` ` as if no one had written on these matters before '' . Nevertheless many elements of Rene_Descartes philosophy have precedents in late Aristotelianism , the revived Stoicism of the 16th century , or in earlier philosophers like Augustine . In Rene_Descartes natural philosophy ,"
"eos In Rene_Descartes natural philosophy , Rene_Descartes differs from the Schools on two major points : first , Rene_Descartes rejects the analysis of corporeal substance into matter and form ; second , Rene_Descartes rejects any appeal to ends - divine or natural - in explaining natural phenomena . In Rene_Descartes theology , Rene_Descartes insists on the absolute freedom of God 's act of creation ."
"eos As the inventor of the Cartesian coordinate system , Rene_Descartes founded analytic geometry , that bridge between algebra and geometry crucial to the invention of the calculus and analysis . Rene_Descartes reflections on mind and mechanism began the strain of western thought that much later , impelled by the invention of the electronic computer and by the possibility of machine intelligence , blossomed into , eg , the Turing test ."
